produced by judith boss an anonymous volunteer and david widger uncle tom_loker cabin or life among the lowly by harriet beecher stowe volume
late in the afternoon of a chilly day in february two gentleman were sitting alone over their wine in a well furnished dining parlor in the town of in kentucky
there were no servant present and the gentleman with chair closely approaching seemed to be discussing some subject with great earnestness
i chapter i in which the reader is introduced to a man of humanity for convenience sake we have said hitherto two gentleman
he was a short thick set man with coarse commonplace features and that swaggering air of pretension which marks a low man who is trying to elbow his way upward in the world
he was much over dressed in a gaudy vest of many colors a blue neckerchief bedropped gayly with yellow spots and arranged with a flaunting tie quite in keeping with the general air of the man
his hand large and coarse were plentifully bedecked with rings and he wore a heavy gold watch chain with a bundle of seals of portentous size and a great variety of colors attached to it which in the ardor of conversation he was in the habit of flourishing and jingling with evident satisfaction
his conversation was in free and easy defiance of murray grammar and was garnished at convenient intervals with various profane expression which not even the desire to be graphic in our account shall induce us to transcribe
one of the party however when critically examined did not seem strictly speaking to come under the species english grammar by lindley murray the most authoritative american grammarian of his day
his companion mr_shelby had the appearance of a gentleman and the arrangements of the house and the general air of the housekeeping indicated easy and even opulent circumstances
as we before stated the two were in the midst of an earnest conversation that is the way i should arrange the matter said mr_shelby
i cant make trade that way i positively cant mr_shelby said the other holding up a glass of wine between his eye and the light
tom_loker is an uncommon fellow he is certainly worth that sum anywhere steady honest capable manages my whole farm like a clock
why the fact is mr_haley you mean honest as nigger go said mr_haley helping himself to a glass of brandy
no i mean really tom_loker is a good steady sensible pious fellow he got religion at a camp meeting four year ago and i believe he really did get it
i ve trusted him since then with everything i have money house horse and let him come and go round the country and i always found him true and square in everything
some folks dont believe there is pious nigger mr_shelby said mr_haley with a candid flourish of his hand but i do
last lot i took to orleanst was as good as a meetin now really to hear that critter pray and he was quite gentle and quiet like
he fetched me a good sum too for i bought him cheap of a man that was bliged to sell out so i realized six hundred on him
i had a fellow now in this yer yes i consider religion a valeyable thing in a nigger when it the genuine article and no mistake
why last fall i let him go to cincinnati alone to do business for me and bring home five hundred dollar
well tom_loker got the real article if ever a fellow had rejoined the other tom_loker says i to him i trust you because i think you re a christian i know you wouldnt cheat
tom_loker comes back sure enough i knew he would some low fellow they say said to him tom_loker why dont you make tracks for canada
ah master trusted me and i couldnt they told me about it i am sorry to part with tom_loker i must say
you ought to let him cover the whole balance of the debt and you would mr_haley if you had any conscience
well i ve got just as much conscience as any man in business can afford to keep just a little you know to swear by ast were said the trader jocularly and then i ready to do anything in reason to blige friend but this yer you see is a leetle too hard on a fellow a leetle too hard
the trader sighed contemplatively and poured out some more brandy well then mr_haley how will you trade said mr_shelby after an uneasy interval of silence
hum none that i could well spare to tell the truth it only hard necessity makes me willing to sell at all
well havent you a boy or gal that you could throw in with tom_loker i dont like parting with any of my hand that a fact
here the door opened and a small quadroon boy between four and five year of age entered the room there was something in his appearance remarkably beautiful and engaging
his black hair fine as floss silk hung in glossy curls about his round dimpled face while a pair of large dark eye full of fire and softness looked out from beneath the rich long lashes as he peered curiously into the apartment
a gay robe of scarlet and yellow plaid carefully made and neatly fitted set off to advantage the dark and rich style of his beauty and a certain comic air of assurance blended with bashfulness showed that he had been not unused to being petted and noticed by his master
hulloa jim_crow said mr_shelby whistling and snapping a bunch of raisins towards him pick that up now
the child scampered with all his little strength after the prize while his master laughed come here jim_crow said he
the child came up and the master patted the curly head and chucked him under the chin now jim_crow show this gentleman how you can dance and sing
the boy commenced one of those wild grotesque songs common among the negroes in a rich clear voice accompanying his singing with many comic evolutions of the hand foot and whole body all in perfect time to the music
bravo said mr_haley throwing him a quarter of an orange now jim_crow walk like old uncle cudjoe when he has the rheumatism said his master
instantly the flexible limbs of the child assumed the appearance of deformity and distortion as with his back humped up and his master stick in his hand he hobbled about the room his childish face drawn into a doleful pucker and spitting from right to left in imitation of an old man
the boy drew his chubby face down to a formidable length and commenced toning a psalm tune through his nose with imperturbable gravity
both gentleman laughed uproariously now jim_crow said his master show us how old elder robbins leads the psalm
tell you what said he suddenly clapping his hand on mr_shelby shoulder fling in that chap and i ll settle the business i will
hurrah bravo what a young un said mr_haley that chap a case i ll promise come now if that aint doing the thing up about the rightest
at this moment the door was pushed gently open and a young quadroon woman apparently about twenty five entered the room there needed only a glance from the child to her to identify her as its mother
the brown of her complexion gave way on the cheek to a perceptible flush which deepened as she saw the gaze of the strange man fixed upon her in bold and undisguised admiration
her dress was of the neatest possible fit and set off to advantage her finely moulded shape a delicately formed hand and a trim foot and ankle were items of appearance that did not escape the quick eye of the trader well used to run up at a glance the points of a fine female article
there was the same rich full dark eye with its long lashes the same ripples of silky black hair well eliza_harris said her master as she stopped and looked hesitatingly at him
i was looking for harry please sir and the boy bounded toward her showing his spoils which he had gathered in the skirt of his robe
well take him away then said mr_shelby and hastily she withdrew carrying the child on her arm
by jupiter said the trader turning to him in admiration there an article now you might make your fortune on that ar gal in orleans any day
i dont want to make my fortune on her said mr_shelby dryly and seeking to turn the conversation he uncorked a bottle of fresh wine and asked his companion opinion of it
i ve seen over a thousand in my day paid down for gal not a bit handsomer capital sir first chop said the trader then turning and slapping his hand familiarly on mr_shelby shoulder
he added come how will you trade about the gal what shall i say for her what ll you take mr_haley she is not to be sold said mr_shelby
my wife would not part with her for her weight in gold ay ay woman always say such thing cause they ha nt no sort of calculation
just show em how many watches feathers and trinkets one weight in gold would buy and that alters the case i reckon
i tell you mr_haley this must not be spoken of i say no and i mean no said mr_shelby decidedly
well you ll let me have the boy though said the trader you must own i ve come down pretty handsomely for him
why i ve got a friend that going into this yer branch of the business wants to buy up handsome boy to raise for the market
what on earth can you want with the child said mr_shelby fancy articles entirely sell for waiters and so on to rich uns that can pay for handsome uns
it sets off one of yer great place a real handsome boy to open door wait and tend they fetch a good sum and this little devil is such a comical musical concern he just the article
i would rather not sell him said mr_shelby thoughtfully the fact is sir i a humane man and i hate to take the boy from his mother sir
you do la yes something of that ar natur i understand perfectly it is mighty onpleasant getting on with woman sometimes i al ays hates these yer screechin screamin time
now what if you get the girl off for a day or a week or so then the thing done quietly all over before she comes home
they are mighty onpleasant but as i manages business i generally avoids em sir your wife might get her some ear rings or a new gown or some such truck to make up with her
i afraid not lor bless ye yes these critters aint like white folks you know they gets over thing only manage right
now they say said mr_haley assuming a candid and confidential air that this kind trade is hardening to the feeling but i never found it so
i ve seen em as would pull a woman child out of her arm and set him up to sell and she screechin like mad all the time very bad policy damages the article makes em quite unfit for service sometimes
fact is i never could do thing up the way some fellers manage the business i knew a real handsome gal once in orleans as was entirely ruined by this sort handling
the fellow that was trading for her didnt want her baby and she was one of your real high sort when her blood was up
it kinder makes my blood run cold to think oft and when they carried off the child and locked her up she jest went ravin mad and died in a week
i tell you she squeezed up her child in her arm and talked and went on real awful clear waste sir of a thousand dollar just for want of management there wheret is
and the trader leaned back in his chair and folded his arm with an air of virtuous decision apparently considering himself a second wilberforce
the subject appeared to interest the gentleman deeply for while mr_shelby was thoughtfully peeling an orange mr_haley broke out afresh with becoming diffidence but as if actually driven by the force of truth to say a few word more
it dont look well now for a feller to be praisin himself but i say it jest because it the truth
i believe i reckoned to bring in about the finest droves of nigger that is brought in at least i ve been told so if i have once i reckon i have a hundred time all in good case fat and likely and i lose as few as any man in the business
and i lays it all to my management sir and humanity sir i may say is the great pillar of my management
it always best to do the humane thing sir that been my experience mr_shelby did not know what to say and so he said indeed
now i ve been laughed at for my notions sir and i ve been talked to they ant pop lar and they ant common but i stuck to em sir
i ve stuck to em and realized well on em yes sir they have paid their passage i may say and the trader laughed at his joke
there was something so piquant and original in these elucidations of humanity that mr_shelby could not help laughing in company
perhaps you laugh too dear reader but you know humanity comes out in a variety of strange form now a day and there is no end to the odd thing that humane people will say and do
mr_shelby laugh encouraged the trader to proceed it strange now but i never could beat this into people head
now there was tom_loker my old partner down in natchez he was a clever fellow tom_loker was only the very devil with nigger on principlet was you see for a better hearted feller never broke breadt was his system sir
why tom_loker i used to say when your gal takes on and cry what the use crackin on em over the head and knockin on em round
i used to talk to tom_loker it ridiculous says i and dont do no sort good why i dont see no harm in their cryin says i it natur says i and
besides tom_loker says i it jest spiles your gal they get sickly and down in the mouth and sometimes they gets ugly particular yallow gal
if natur cant blow off one way it will another do and it the devil and all gettin on em broke in
depend on it tom_loker a little humanity thrown in along goes a heap further than all your jawin and crackin and it pays better says i depend ont
but tom_loker couldnt get the hang ont and he spiled so many for me that i had to break off with him though he was a good hearted fellow and as fair a business hand as is goin
now says i why cant you kinder coax em up and speak em fair and do you find your way of managing do the business better than tom_loker said mr_shelby
you see when i any way can i takes a leetle care about the onpleasant part like selling young uns and that get the gal out of the way out of sight out of mind you know and when it clean done and cant be helped they naturally gets used to it
tant you know as if it was white folks that brought up in the way of spectin to keep their child and wife and all that
nigger you know that fetched up properly ha nt no kind of spectations of no kind so all these thing comes easier
why yes sir i may say so i afraid mine are not properly brought up then said mr_shelby
now a nigger you see what got to be hacked and tumbled round the world and sold to tom_loker and dick and the lord knows who tant no kindness to be givin on him notions and expectations and bringin on him up too well for the rough and tumble comes all the harder on him arter
now i venture to say your nigger would be quite chop fallen in a place where some of your plantation nigger would be singing and whooping like all possessed
every man you know mr_shelby naturally thinks well of his own way and i think i treat nigger just about as well as it ever worth while to treat em
pose not you kentucky folks spile your nigger you mean well by em but tant no real kindness arter all
it a happy thing to be satisfied said mr_shelby with a slight shrug and some perceptible feeling of a disagreeable nature
well said mr_haley after they had both silently picked their nuts for a season what do you say i ll think the matter over and talk with my wife said mr_shelby
meantime mr_haley if you want the matter carried on in the quiet way you speak of you best not let your business in this neighborhood be known
it will get out among my boy and it will not be a particularly quiet business getting away any of my fellow if they know it i ll promise you
i in a devil of a hurry and shall want to know as soon as possible what i may depend on said he rising and putting on his overcoat
well call up this evening between six and seven and you shall have my answer said mr_shelby and the trader bowed himself out of the apartment
i like to have been able to kick the fellow down the steps said he to himself as he saw the door fairly closed with his impudent assurance but he knows how much he has me at advantage
if anybody had ever said to me that i should sell tom_loker down south to one of those rascally trader i should have said is thy servant a dog that he should do this thing
certainly by all means mum of course but i ll tell you and now it must come for aught i see
and eliza_harris child too i know that i shall have some fuss with wife about that and for that matter about tom_loker too
so much for being in debt heigho the fellow sees his advantage and means to push it perhaps the mildest form of the system of slavery is to be seen in the state of kentucky
the general prevalence of agricultural pursuits of a quiet and gradual nature not requiring those periodic seasons of hurry and pressure that are called for in the business of more southern districts makes the task of the negro a more healthful and reasonable one while the master content with a more gradual style of acquisition has not those temptations to hardheartedness which always overcome frail human nature when the prospect of sudden and rapid gain is weighed in the balance with no heavier counterpoise than the interests of the helpless and unprotected
whoever visits some estates there and witnesses the good humored indulgence of some master and mistress and the affectionate loyalty of some slave might be tempted to dream the oft fabled poetic legend of a patriarchal institution and all that but over and above the scene there broods a portentous shadow the shadow of law
so long as the law considers all these human beings with beating heart and living affections only as so many thing belonging to a master so long as the failure or misfortune or imprudence or death of the kindest owner may cause them any day to exchange a life of kind protection and indulgence for one of hopeless misery and toil so long it is impossible to make anything beautiful or desirable in the best regulated administration of slavery
mr_shelby was a fair average kind of man good natured and kindly and disposed to easy indulgence of those around him and there had never been a lack of anything which might contribute to the physical comfort of the negroes on his estate
he had however speculated largely and quite loosely had involved himself deeply and his notes to a large amount had come into the hand of mr_haley and this small piece of information is the key to the preceding conversation
now it had so happened that in approaching the door eliza_harris had caught enough of the conversation to know that a trader was making offers to her master for somebody
she would gladly have stopped at the door to listen as she came out but her mistress just then calling she was obliged to hasten away
her heart swelled and throbbed and she involuntarily strained him so tight that the little fellow looked up into her face in astonishment
eliza_harris girl what ails you today said her mistress when eliza_harris had upset the wash pitcher knocked down the workstand and finally was abstractedly offering her mistress a long nightgown in place of the silk dress she had ordered her to bring from the wardrobe
still she thought she heard the trader make an offer for her boy could she be mistaken eliza_harris started missis
she said raising her eye then bursting into tear she sat down in a chair and began sobbing why eliza_harris child what ails you said her mistress
missis missis said eliza_harris there been a trader talking with master in the parlor i heard him well silly child suppose there has
missis do you suppose mas would sell my harry and the poor creature threw herself into a chair and sobbed convulsively
you know your master never deals with those southern trader and never means to sell any of his servant as long as they behave well
sell him no you foolish girl why you silly child who do you think would want to buy your harry do you think all the world are set on him as you are you goosie
there now put my back hair up in that pretty braid you learnt the other day and dont go listening at door any more
come cheer up and hook my dress well but missis you never would give your consent to to nonsense child to be sure i shouldnt
what do you talk so for i would as soon have one of my own child sold but really eliza_harris you are getting altogether too proud of that little fellow
reassured by her mistress confident tone eliza_harris proceeded nimbly and adroitly with her toilet laughing at her own fears as she proceeded
a man cant put his nose into the door but you think he must be coming to buy him mrs mr_shelby was a woman of high class both intellectually and morally
to that natural magnanimity and generosity of mind which one often marks as characteristic of the woman of kentucky she added high moral and religious sensibility and principle carried out with great energy and ability into practical results
her husband who made no professions to any particular religious character nevertheless reverenced and respected the consistency of hers and stood perhaps a little in awe of her opinion
certain it was that he gave her unlimited scope in all her benevolent efforts for the comfort instruction and improvement of her servant though he never took any decided part in them himself
in fact if not exactly a believer in the doctrine of the efficiency of the extra good work of saints he really seemed somehow or other to fancy that his wife had piety and benevolence enough for two to indulge a shadowy expectation of getting into heaven through her superabundance of qualities to which he made no particular pretension
the heaviest load on his mind after his conversation with the trader lay in the foreseen necessity of breaking to his wife the arrangement contemplated meeting the importunities and opposition which he knew he should have reason to encounter
mrs mr_shelby being entirely ignorant of her husband embarrassments and knowing only the general kindliness of his temper had been quite sincere in the entire incredulity with which she had met eliza_harris suspicions
in fact she dismissed the matter from her mind without a second thought and being occupied in preparations for an evening visit it passed out of her thoughts entirely
the traveller in the south must often have remarked that peculiar air of refinement that softness of voice and manner which seems in many case to be a particular gift to the quadroon and mulatto woman
these natural graces in the quadroon are often united with beauty of the most dazzling kind and in almost every case with a personal appearance prepossessing and agreeable
eliza_harris such as we have described her is not a fancy sketch but taken from remembrance as we saw her year ago in kentucky
safe under the protecting care of her mistress eliza_harris had reached maturity without those temptations which make beauty so fatal an inheritance to a slave
she had been married to a bright and talented young mulatto man who was a slave on a neighboring estate and bore the name of george_harris
this young man had been hired out by his master to work in a bagging factory where his adroitness and ingenuity caused him to be considered the first hand in the place
he had invented a machine for the cleaning of the hemp which considering the education and circumstances of the inventor displayed quite as much mechanical genius as whitney cotton gin
chapter ii the mother eliza_harris had been brought up by her mistress from girlhood as a petted and indulged favorite
a machine of this description was really the invention of a young colored man in kentucky mrs stowe note he was possessed of a handsome person and pleasing manner and was a general favorite in the factory
nevertheless as this young man was in the eye of the law not a man but a thing all these superior qualifications were subject to the control of a vulgar narrow minded tyrannical master
this same gentleman having heard of the fame of george_harris invention took a ride over to the factory to see what this intelligent chattel had been about
he was waited upon over the factory shown the machinery by george_harris who in high spirit talked so fluently held himself so erect looked so handsome and manly that his master began to feel an uneasy consciousness of inferiority
he was received with great enthusiasm by the employer who congratulated him on possessing so valuable a slave what business had his slave to be marching round the country inventing machines and holding up his head among gentleman
he soon put a stop to it he take him back and put him to hoeing and digging and see if he step about so smart
accordingly the manufacturer and all hand concerned were astounded when he suddenly demanded george_harris wages and announced his intention of taking him home
but mr george_harris remonstrated the manufacturer isnt this rather sudden what if it is isnt the man mine
we would be willing sir to increase the rate of compensation no object at all sir i dont need to hire any of my hand out unless i ve a mind to
but sir he seems peculiarly adapted to this business dare say he may be never was much adapted to anything that i set him about i ll be bound
but only think of his inventing this machine interposed one of the workmen rather unluckily yes a machine for saving work is it
he invent that i ll be bound let a nigger alone for that any time they are all labor saving machines themselves every one of em
george_harris had stood like one transfixed at hearing his doom thus suddenly pronounced by a power that he knew was irresistible
he folded his arm tightly pressed in his lips but a whole volcano of bitter feeling burned in his bosom and sent streams of fire through his veins
he breathed short and his large dark eye flashed like live coals and he might have broken out into some dangerous ebullition had not the kindly manufacturer touched him on the arm and said in a low tone give way george_harris go with him for the present
the tyrant observed the whisper and conjectured its import though he could not hear what was said and he inwardly strengthened himself in his determination to keep the power he possessed over his victim
no he shall tramp we ll try to help you yet george_harris was taken home and put to the meanest drudgery of the farm
he had been able to repress every disrespectful word but the flashing eye the gloomy and troubled brow were part of a natural language that could not be repressed indubitable signs which showed too plainly that the man could not become a thing
it was during the happy period of his employment in the factory that george_harris had seen and married his wife during that period being much trusted and favored by his employer he had free liberty to come and go at discretion
the marriage was highly approved of by mrs mr_shelby who with a little womanly complacency in match making felt pleased to unite her handsome favorite with one of her own class who seemed in every way suited to her and so they were married in her mistress great parlor and her mistress herself adorned the bride beautiful hair with orange blossoms and threw over it
the bridal veil which certainly could scarce have rested on a fairer head and there was no lack of white gloves and cake and wine of admiring guests to praise the bride beauty and her mistress indulgence and liberality
for a year or two eliza_harris saw her husband frequently and there was nothing to interrupt their happiness except the loss of two infant child to whom she was passionately attached and whom she mourned with a grief so intense as to call for gentle remonstrance from her mistress who sought with maternal anxiety to direct her naturally passionate feeling within the bounds of reason and religion
after the birth of little harry however she had gradually become tranquillized and settled and every bleeding tie and throbbing nerve once more entwined with that little life seemed to become sound and healthful and eliza_harris was a happy woman up to the time that her husband was rudely torn from his kind employer and brought under the iron sway of his legal owner
the manufacturer true to his word visited mr george_harris a week or two after george_harris had been taken away when as he hoped the heat of the occasion had passed away and tried every possible inducement to lead him to restore him to his former employment
you neednt trouble yourself to talk any longer said he doggedly i know my own business sir i did not presume to interfere with it sir
i only thought that you might think it for your interest to let your man to us on the terms proposed
i saw your winking and whispering the day i took him out of the factory but you dont come it over me that way
i understand the matter well enough it a free country sir the man mine and i do what i please with him that it
and so fell george_harris last hope nothing before him but a life of toil and drudgery rendered more bitter by every little smarting vexation and indignity which tyrannical ingenuity could devise
a very humane jurist once said the worst use you can put a man to is to hang him no there is another use that a man can be put to that is worse
the husband and father mrs mr_shelby had gone on her visit and eliza_harris stood in the verandah rather dejectedly looking after the retreating carriage when a hand was laid on her shoulder
chapter iii she turned and a bright smile lighted up her fine eye george_harris is it you how you frightened me
missis is gone to spend the afternoon so come into my little room and we ll have the time all to ourselves
saying this she drew him into a neat little apartment opening on the verandah where she generally sat at her sewing within call of her mistress
well i am so glad you come how glad i am why dont you smile and look at harry how he grows
the boy stood shyly regarding his father through his curls holding close to the skirts of his mother dress
isnt he beautiful said eliza_harris lifting his long curls and kissing him i wish he never been born said george_harris bitterly
i wish i never been born myself surprised and frightened eliza_harris sat down leaned her head on her husband shoulder and burst into tear
there now eliza_harris it too bad for me to make you feel so poor girl said he fondly it too bad how i wish you never had seen me you might have been happy
george_harris george how can you talk so what dreadful thing has happened or is going to happen i sure we ve been very happy till lately
then drawing his child on his knee he gazed intently on his glorious dark eye and passed his hand through his long curls
just like you eliza_harris and you are the handsomest woman i ever saw and the best one i ever wish to see but oh i wish i never seen you nor you me
so we have dear said george_harris george how can you yes eliza_harris it all misery misery misery
my life is bitter as wormwood the very life is burning out of me i a poor miserable forlorn drudge i shall only drag you down with me that all
what the use of our trying to do anything trying to know anything trying to be anything what the use of living
i know how you feel about losing your place in the factory and you have a hard master but pray be patient and perhaps something patient said he interrupting her havent i been patient
did i say a word when he came and took me away for no earthly reason from the place where everybody was kind to me
i wish i was dead now dear george_harris that is really wicked i paid him truly every cent of my
earnings and they all say i worked well well it is dreadful said eliza_harris but after all he is your master you know
my master and who made him my master that what i think of what right has he to me i a man as much as he is
i know more about business than he does i am a better manager than he is i can read better than he can i can write a better hand and
i ve learned it all myself and no thanks to him i ve learned it in spite of him and now what right has he to make a dray horse of me to take me from thing i can do and do better than he can and put me to work that any horse can do
he tries to do it he says he ll bring me down and humble me and he puts me to just the hardest meanest and dirtiest work on purpose
i a better man than he is george_harris george you frighten me why i never heard you talk so i afraid you ll do something dreadful
i dont wonder at your feeling at all but oh do be careful do do for my sake for harry i have been careful and i have been patient but it growing worse and worse
i thought i could do my work well and keep on quiet and have some time to read and learn out of work hour but the more he sees i can do the more he loads on
he says that though i dont say anything he sees i ve got the devil in me and he means to bring it out and one of these day it will come out in a way that he wont like or i mistaken
flesh and blood cant bear it any longer every chance he can get to insult and torment me he takes dear
it was only yesterday said george_harris as i was busy loading stones into a cart that young mas tom_loker stood there slashing his whip so near the horse that the creature was frightened
what shall we do said eliza_harris mournfully i asked him to stop as pleasant as i could he just kept right on
i held his hand and then he screamed and kicked and ran to his father and told him that i was fighting him
he came in a rage and said he teach me who was my master and he tied me to a tree and cut switches for young master and told him that he might whip me till he was tired and he did do it
if i dont make him remember it some time and the brow of the young man grew dark and his eye burned with an expression that made his young wife tremble
i begged him again and then he turned on me and began striking me who made this man my master
well said eliza_harris mournfully i always thought that i must obey my master and mistress or i couldnt be a christian
there is some sense in it in your case they have brought you up like a child fed you clothed you indulged you and taught you so that you have a good education that is some reason why they should claim you
but i have been kicked and cuffed and sworn at and at the best only let alone and what do i owe
that what i want to know he said i ve paid for all my keeping a hundred time over
i wont bear it no i wont he said clenching his hand with a fierce frown eliza_harris trembled and was silent
she had never seen her husband in this mood before and her gentle system of ethics seemed to bend like a reed in the surges of such passions
you know poor little carlo that you gave me added george_harris the creature has been about all the comfort that i ve had
he has slept with me night and followed me around day and kind looked at me as if he understood how i felt
well the other day i was just feeding him with a few old scraps i picked up by the kitchen door and mas came along and said i was feeding him up at his expense and that he couldnt afford to have every nigger keeping his dog and ordered me to tie a stone to his neck and throw him in the pond
george_harris you didnt do it do it not i but he did mas and tom_loker pelted the poor drowning creature with stones
poor thing he looked at me so mournful as if he wondered why i didnt save him i had to take a flogging because i wouldnt do it myself
i dont care mas will find out that i one that whipping wont tame my day will come yet if he dont look out
what are you going to do george_harris dont do anything wicked if you only trust in god and try to do right he ll deliver you
i ant a christian like you eliza_harris my heart full of bitterness i cant trust in god why does he let thing be so
george_harris we must have faith mistress says that when all thing go wrong to us we must believe that god is doing the very best
that easy to say for people that are sitting on their sofas and riding in their carriages but let em be where i am i guess it would come some harder
i wish i could be good but my heart burns and cant be reconciled anyhow you couldnt in my place you cant now if i tell you all i ve got to say
well lately mas has been saying that he was a fool to let me marry off the place that he hates mr_shelby and all his tribe because they are proud and hold their head up above him and that i ve got proud notions from you and he says he wont let me come here any more and that i shall take a wife and settle down on his place
at first he only scolded and grumbled these thing but yesterday he told me that i should take mina for a wife and settle down in a cabin with her or he would sell me down river
why but you were married to me by the minister as much as if you been a white man said eliza_harris simply
you dont know the whole yet what can be coming now dont you know a slave cant be married
there is no law in this country for that i cant hold you for my wife if he chooses to part us
i wish i never been born it would have been better for us both it would have been better for this poor child if he had never been born
that why i wish i never seen you why all this may happen to him yet but master is so kind
yes but who knows he may die and then he may be sold to nobody knows who what pleasure is it that he is handsome and smart and bright
i tell you eliza_harris that a sword will pierce through your soul for every good and pleasant thing your child is or has it will make him worth too much for you to keep
the word smote heavily on eliza_harris heart the vision of the trader came before her eye and as if some one had struck her a deadly blow she turned pale and gasped for breath
she looked nervously out on the verandah where the boy tired of the grave conversation had retired and where he was riding triumphantly up and down on mr_shelby walking stick
she would have spoken to tell her husband her fears but checked herself no no he has enough to bear poor fellow
she thought no i wont tell him besides it ant true missis never deceives us so eliza_harris my girl said the husband mournfully bear up now and good by for i going
to canada said he straightening himself up and when i there i ll buy you that all the hope that left us
going george_harris going where you have a kind master that wont refuse to sell you i ll buy you and the boy god helping me i will
dreadful if you should be taken i wont be taken eliza_harris i ll die first i ll be free or i ll die
you wont kill yourself no need of that they will kill me fast enough they never will get me down the river alive
george_harris for my sake do be careful dont do anything wicked dont lay hand on yourself or anybody else you are tempted too much too much but dont go you must but go carefully prudently pray god to help you
mas took it into his head to send me right by here with a note to mr symmes that life a mile past
well then eliza_harris hear my plan i believe he expected i should come here to tell you what i have
it would please him if he thought it would aggravate mr_shelby folks as he calls em i going home quite resigned you understand as if all was over
there are those that will help me and in the course of a week or so i shall be among the missing some day
i ve got some preparations made and pray for me eliza_harris perhaps the good lord will hear you pray yourself george_harris and go trusting in him then you wont do anything wicked
they stood silent then there were last word and sobs and bitter weeping such parting as those may make whose hope to meet again is as the spider web and the husband and wife were parted
well now good by said george_harris holding eliza_harris hand and gazing into her eye without moving chapter iv an evening in
the cabin of uncle tom_loker was a small log building close adjoining to the house as the negro par excellence designates his master dwelling
in front it had a neat garden patch where every summer strawberries raspberries and a variety of fruits and vegetables flourished under careful tending
the whole front of it was covered by a large scarlet bignonia and a native multiflora rose which entwisting and interlacing left scarce a vestige of the rough logs to be seen
here also in summer various brilliant annuals such as marigolds petunias four clocks found an indulgent corner in which to unfold their splendors and were the delight and pride of aunt_chloe heart
the evening meal at the house is over and aunt_chloe who presided over its preparation as head cook has left to inferior officers in the kitchen the business of clearing away and washing dishes and come out into her own snug territories to get her ole man supper therefore doubt not that it is her you see by the fire presiding with anxious interest over certain frizzling items in a stew pan and anon with grave consideration lifting the cover of a bake kettle from whence steam forth indubitable intimations of something good
a round black shining face is hers so glossy as to suggest the idea that she might have been washed over with white of eggs like one of her own tea rusks
her whole plump countenance beams with satisfaction and contentment from under her well starched checked turban bearing on it however if we must confess it a little of that tinge of self consciousness which becomes the first cook of the neighborhood as aunt_chloe was universally held and acknowledged to be
uncle tom_loker cabin let us enter the dwelling a cook she certainly was in the very bone and centre of her soul
not a chicken or turkey or duck in the barn yard but looked grave when they saw her approaching and seemed evidently to be reflecting on their latter end and certain it was that she was always meditating on trussing stuffing and roasting to a degree that was calculated to inspire terror in any reflecting fowl living
her corn cake in all its varieties of hoe cake dodgers muffins and other species too numerous to mention was a sublime mystery to all less practised compounders and she would shake her fat side with honest pride and merriment as she would narrate the fruitless efforts that one and another of her compeers had made to attain to her elevation
the arrival of company at the house the arranging of dinners and suppers in style awoke all the energies of her soul and no sight was more welcome to her than a pile of travelling trunks launched on the verandah for
just at present however aunt_chloe is looking into the bake pan in which congenial operation we shall leave her till we finish our picture of the cottage
in one corner of it stood a bed covered neatly with a snowy spread and by the side of it was a piece of carpeting of some considerable size
on this piece of carpeting aunt_chloe took her stand as being decidedly in the upper walks of life and it and the bed by which it lay and the whole corner in fact were treated with distinguished consideration and made so far as possible sacred from the marauding inroads and desecrations of little folks
then she foresaw fresh efforts and fresh triumphs in fact that corner was the drawing room of the establishment in the other corner was a bed of much humbler pretensions and evidently designed for use
the wall over the fireplace was adorned with some very brilliant scriptural prints and a portrait of general washington drawn and colored in a manner which would certainly have astonished that hero if ever he happened to meet with its like
on a rough bench in the corner a couple of woolly headed boy with glistening black eye and fat shining cheeks were busy in superintending the first walking operations of the baby which as is usually the case consisted in getting up on its foot balancing a moment and then tumbling down each successive failure being violently cheered as something decidedly clever
a table somewhat rheumatic in its limbs was drawn out in front of the fire and covered with a cloth displaying cups and saucers of a decidedly brilliant pattern with other symptoms of an approaching meal
at this table was seated uncle tom_loker mr_shelby best hand who as he is to be the hero of our story we must daguerreotype for our readers
he was a large broad chested powerfully made man of a full glossy black and a face whose truly african features were characterized by an expression of grave and steady good sense united with much kindliness and benevolence
he was very busily intent at this moment on a slate lying before him on which he was carefully and slowly endeavoring to accomplish a copy of some letter in which operation he was overlooked by young mas george_harris a smart bright boy of thirteen who appeared fully to realize the dignity of his position as instructor
there was something about his whole air self respecting and dignified yet united with a confiding and humble simplicity not that way uncle tom_loker not that way
said he briskly as uncle tom_loker laboriously brought up the tail of his the wrong side out that makes a you see
la sakes now does it said uncle tom_loker looking with a respectful admiring air as his young teacher flourishingly scrawled s and s innumerable for his edification and then taking the pencil in his big heavy fingers he patiently recommenced
how easy white folks al us does thing said aunt_chloe pausing while she was greasing a griddle with a scrap of bacon on her fork and regarding young master george_harris with pride
the way he can write now and read too and then to come out here evening and read his lessons to us it mighty interestin
but aunt_chloe i getting mighty hungry said george_harris isnt that cake in the skillet almost done mose done mas george_harris said aunt_chloe lifting the lid and peeping in browning beautiful a real lovely brown
ah let me alone for dat missis let sally try to make some caket other day jes to larn her she said
o go way missis said i it really hurts my feelin now to see good vittles spilt dat ar way cake ris all to one side no shape at all no more than my shoe go way
and with this final expression of contempt for sally greenness aunt_chloe whipped the cover off the bake kettle and disclosed to view a neatly baked pound cake of which no city confectioner need to have been ashamed
this being evidently the central point of the entertainment aunt_chloe began now to bustle about earnestly in the supper department
here you mose and pete get out de way you nigger get away polly honey mammy ll give her baby some fin by and by
now mas george_harris you jest take off dem book and set down now with my old man and i ll take up de sausages and have de first griddle full of cakes on your plates in less dan no time

so you did so you did honey said aunt_chloe heaping the smoking batter cakes on his plate you know your old aunty keep the best for you
and with that aunty gave george_harris a nudge with her finger designed to be immensely facetious and turned again to her griddle with great briskness
now for the cake said mas george_harris when the activity of the griddle department had somewhat subsided and with that the youngster flourished a large knife over the article in question
o let you alone for dat go way la bless you mas george_harris said aunt_chloe with earnestness catching his arm you wouldnt be for cuttin it wid
dat ar great heavy knife smash all down spile all de pretty rise of it here i ve got a thin old knife i keeps sharp a purpose
dar now see comes apart light as a feather now eat away you wont get anything to beat dat ar tom_loker lincon says said george_harris speaking with his mouth full that their jinny is a better cook than you
they spectable folks enough in a kinder plain way but as to gettin up anything in style they dont begin to have a notion on
dem lincons ant much count no way said aunt_chloe contemptuously i mean set along side our folkst set
mas lincon now alongside mas mr_shelby good lor and missis lincon can she kinder sweep it into a room like my missis so kinder splendid yer know
o go way dont tell me nothing of dem lincons and aunt_chloe tossed her head as one who hoped she did know something of the world
well though i ve heard you say said george_harris that jinny was a pretty fair cook so i did said aunt_chloe i may say dat
good plain common cookin jinny ll do make a good pone bread bile her taters far her corn cakes isnt extra not extra now jinny corn cakes isnt but then they far but
lor come to de higher branches and what can she do why she makes pies sartin she does but what kinder crust
now i went over thar when miss mary was gwine to be married and jinny she jest showed me de weddin pies
can she make your real flecky paste as melts in your mouth and lies all up like a puff jinny and i is good friend ye know
i never said nothing but go long mas george_harris why i shouldnt sleep a wink for a week if i had a batch of pies like dem ar
why dey want no countt all i suppose jinny thought they were ever so nice said george_harris thought so didn t
she thar she was showing em as innocent ye see it jest here jinny dont know lor the family ant nothing
she cant be spected to know ta nt no fault hem ah mas george_harris you doesnt know half your privileges in yer family and bringin up
here aunt_chloe sighed and rolled up her eye with emotion i sure aunt_chloe i understand my pie and pudding privileges said george_harris
aunt_chloe sat back in her chair and indulged in a hearty guffaw of laughter at this witticism of young mas s laughing till the tear rolled down her black shining cheeks and varying the exercise with playfully slapping and poking mas georgey and telling him to go way and that he was a case that he was fit to kill her and that he sartin would kill her one of these day and between each of these sanguinary predictions going off into a laugh each longer and stronger than the other till george_harris really began to think that he was a very dangerously witty fellow and that it became him to be careful how he talked as funny as he could
ask tom_loker lincon if i dont crow over him every time i meet him and so ye telled tom_loker did ye
o lor what young uns will be up ter ye crowed over tom_loker lor mas george_harris if ye wouldnt make a hornbug laugh
yes said george_harris i says to him tom_loker you ought to see some of aunt_chloe pies they re the right sort says i

ye oughter just ask him here to dinner some these time mas george_harris she added it would look quite pretty of ye

lor to think of some of our dinners yer mind dat ar great chicken pie i made when we guv de dinner to general knox

but sometimes when a body has de heaviest kind sponsibility on em as ye may say and is all kinder seris and taken up dey takes dat
now missis she wanted me to do dis way and she wanted me to do dat way and finally i got kinder sarcy and says i now missis do jist look at dem beautiful white hand yourn with long fingers and all a sparkling with rings like my white lilies when de dew on em and look at my great black stumpin hand
now dont ye think dat de lord must have meant me to make de pie crust and you to stay in de parlor

say why she kinder larfed in her eye dem great handsome eye hern and says she well aunt_chloe i think you are about in the right ont says she and she went off in de parlor

lor i was fit to split myself and de gineral he knows what cookin is said aunt_chloe drawing herself up with an air
bery nice man de gineral he comes of one of de bery fustest family in old virginny he knows what what now as well as i do de gineral
ye see there pints in all pies mas george_harris but tant everybody knows what they is or as orter be but the gineral he knows i knew by his marks he made
by this time master george_harris had arrived at that pass to which even a boy can come under uncommon circumstances when he really could not eat another morsel and therefore he was at leisure to notice the pile of woolly head and glistening eye which were regarding their operations hungrily from the opposite corner
yes he knows what de pints is here you mose pete he said breaking off liberal bits and throwing it at them you want some dont you
and george_harris and tom_loker moved to a comfortable seat in the chimney corner while aunte aunt_chloe after baking a goodly pile of cakes took her baby on her lap and began alternately filling its mouth and her own and distributing to mose and pete who seemed rather to prefer eating theirs as they rolled about on the floor under the table tickling each other and occasionally pulling the baby toes
o go long will ye said the mother giving now and then a kick in a kind of general way under the table when the movement became too obstreperous

stop dat ar now will ye better mind yerselves or i ll take ye down a button hole lower when mas george_harris is gone
what meaning was couched under this terrible threat it is difficult to say but certain it is that its awful indistinctness seemed to produce very little impression on the young sinners addressed
la now said uncle tom_loker they are so full of tickle all the while they cant behave theirselves
here the boy emerged from under the table and with hand and face well plastered with molasses began a vigorous kissing of the baby
get along wid ye said the mother pushing away their woolly head ye ll all stick together and never get clar if ye do dat fashion
she said seconding her exhortations by a slap which resounded very formidably but which seemed only to knock out so much more laugh from the young one as they tumbled precipitately over each other out of door where they fairly screamed with merriment
did ye ever see such aggravating young uns said aunt_chloe rather complacently as producing an old towel kept for such emergencies she poured a little water out of the cracked tea pot on it and began rubbing off the molasses from the baby face and hand and having polished her till she shone she set her down in tom_loker lap while she busied herself in clearing away supper
the baby employed the intervals in pulling tom_loker nose scratching his face and burying her fat hand in his woolly hair which last operation seemed to afford her special content
aint she a peart young un said tom_loker holding her from him to take a full length view then getting up he set her on his broad shoulder and began capering and dancing with her while mas george_harris snapped at her with his pocket handkerchief and mose and pete now returned again roared after her like bears till aunt_chloe declared that they fairly took her head off with their noise
as according to her own statement this surgical operation was a matter of daily occurrence in the cabin the declaration no whit abated the merriment till every one had roared and tumbled and danced themselves down to a state of composure

aunt_chloe having thus saved appearances seemed highly delighted to push the thing under saying as she did so well mebbet will do em some good
we likes em the house now resolved itself into a committee of the whole to consider the accommodations and arrangements for the meeting
as the meeting had been held at uncle tom_loker weekly for an indefinite length of time without any more cheers there seemed some encouragement to hope that a way would be discovered at present

during this aside between mose and pete two empty casks had been rolled into the cabin and being secured from rolling by stones on each side boards were laid across them which arrangement together with the turning down of certain tubs and pails and the disposing of the rickety chair at last completed the preparation
george_harris is such a beautiful reader now i know he ll stay to read for us said aunt_chloe pears liket will be so much more interestin
mas george_harris very readily consented for your boy is always ready for anything that makes him of importance
the room was soon filled with a motley assemblage from the old gray headed patriarch of eighty to the young girl and lad of fifteen
a little harmless gossip ensued on various themes such as where old aunt sally got her new red headkerchief and how missis was a going to give lizzy that spotted muslin gown when she got her new berage made up and how mas mr_shelby was thinking of buying a new sorrel colt that was going to prove an addition to the glories of the place
a few of the worshippers belonged to family hard by who had got permission to attend and who brought in various choice scraps of information about the sayings and doings at the house and on the place which circulated as freely as the same sort of small change does in higher circles
not even all the disadvantage of nasal intonation could prevent the effect of the naturally fine voice in air at once wild and spirited
the word were sometimes the well known and common hymns sung in the churches about and sometimes of a wilder more indefinite character picked up at camp meetings
after a while the singing commenced to the evident delight of all present the chorus of one of them which ran as follows was sung with great energy and unction
die on the field of battle die on the field of battle glory in my soul another special favorite had oft repeated the word
i going to glory wont you come along with me dont you see the angels beck ning and a calling me away
there were others which made incessant mention of jordan banks and canaan fields and the new jerusalem for the negro mind impassioned and imaginative always attaches itself to hymns and expression of a vivid and pictorial nature and as they sung some laughed and some cried and some clapped hand or shook hand rejoicingly with each other as if they had fairly gained the other side of the river
dont you see the golden city and the everlasting day various exhortations or relations of experience followed and intermingled with the singing
one old gray headed woman long past work but much revered as a sort of chronicle of the past rose and leaning on her staff said well
well i mighty glad to hear ye all and see ye all once more cause i dont know when i ll be gone to glory but i ve done got ready chil en pears like i got my little bundle all tied up and my bonnet on jest a waitin for the stage to come along and take me home sometimes in the night i think i hear the wheels a rattlin and i lookin out all the time now you jest be ready too for i tell ye all chil en she said striking her staff hard on the floor dat ar glory is a mighty thing
and the old creature sat down with streaming tear as wholly overcome while the whole circle struck up canaan bright canaan i bound for the land of canaan
chil en it a mighty thing chil en you don no nothing about it it wonderful mas george_harris by request read the last chapters of revelation often interrupted by such exclamations as the sakes now
george_harris who was a bright boy and well trained in religious thing by his mother finding himself an object of general admiration threw in expositions of his own from time to time with a commendable seriousness and gravity for which he was admired by the young and blessed by the old and it was agreed on all hand that a minister couldnt lay it off better than he did thatt was reely mazin
only hear that jest think ont is all that a comin sure enough uncle tom_loker was a sort of patriarch in religious matter in the neighborhood
having naturally an organization in which the morale was strongly predominant together with a greater breadth and cultivation of mind than obtained among his companions he was looked up to with great respect as a sort of minister among them and the simple hearty sincere style of his exhortations might have edified even better educated persons
nothing could exceed the touching simplicity the childlike earnestness of his prayer enriched with the language of scripture which seemed so entirely to have wrought itself into his being as to have become a part of himself and to drop from his lips unconsciously in the language of a pious old negro he prayed right up
and so much did his prayer always work on the devotional feeling of his audiences that there seemed often a danger that it would be lost altogether in the abundance of the responses which broke out everywhere around him
while this scene was passing in the cabin of the man one quite otherwise passed in the halls of the master
the trader and mr_shelby were seated together in the dining room afore named at a table covered with paper and writing utensils
mr_shelby was busy in counting some bundles of bills which as they were counted he pushed over to the trader who counted them likewise
but it was in prayer that he especially excelled all fair said the trader and now for signing these yer
mr_shelby hastily drew the bills of sale towards him and signed them like a man that hurries over some disagreeable business and then pushed them over with the money
mr_haley produced from a well worn valise a parchment which after looking over it a moment he handed to mr_shelby who took it with a gesture of suppressed eagerness
wal now the thing done said the trader getting up it done said mr_shelby in a musing tone and fetching a long breath he repeated it done
mr_haley said mr_shelby i hope you ll remember that you promised on your honor you wouldnt sell tom_loker without knowing what sort of hand he going into

circumstances you well know obliged me said mr_shelby haughtily wal you know they may blige me too said the trader
howsomever i ll do the very best i can in gettin tom_loker a good berth as to my treatin on him bad you neednt be a grain afeard
after the expositions which the trader had previously given of his humane principles mr_shelby did not feel particularly reassured by these declarations but as they were the best comfort the case admitted of he allowed the trader to depart in silence and betook himself to a solitary cigar
if there anything that i thank the lord for it is that i never noways cruel chapter showing the feeling of living property on changing
he was lounging in a large easy chair looking over some letter that had come in the afternoon mail and she was standing before her mirror brushing out the complicated braids and curls in which eliza_harris had arranged her hair for noticing her pale cheeks and haggard eye she had excused her attendance that night and ordered her to bed
the employment naturally enough suggested her conversation with the girl in the morning and turning to her husband she said carelessly by the by arthur who was that low bred fellow that you lugged in to our dinner table today
mr_haley is his name said mr_shelby turning himself rather uneasily in his chair and continuing with his eye fixed on a letter

i have agreed to sell tom_loker and harry both and i dont know why i am to be rated as if i were a monster for doing what every one does every day
well since you must know all it is so but why of all others choose these said mrs mr_shelby
why sell them of all on the place if you must sell at all because they will bring the highest sum of any that why
i could choose another if you say so the fellow made me a high bid on eliza_harris if that would suit you any better said mr_shelby
the wretch said mrs mr_shelby vehemently well i didnt listen to it a moment out of regard to your feeling

i do believe mr_shelby that if he were put to it he would lay down his life for you i know it i dare
say but what the use of all this i cant help myself why not make a pecuniary sacrifice i willing to bear my part of the inconvenience
o mr_shelby i have tried tried most faithfully as a christian woman should to do my duty to these poor simple dependent creature
i have cared for them instructed them watched over them and know all their little care and joys for year and how can i ever hold up my head again among them if for the sake of a little paltry gain we sell such a faithful excellent confiding creature as poor tom_loker and tear from him in a moment all we have taught him to love and value
i have taught them the duties of the family of parent and child and husband and wife and how can i bear to have this open acknowledgment that we care for no tie no duty
i have talked with eliza_harris about her boy her duty to him as a christian mother to watch over him pray for him and bring him up in a christian way and now what can i say if you tear him away and sell him soul and body to a profane unprincipled man just to save a little money
i have told her that one soul is worth more than all the money in the world and how will she believe me when she sees us turn round and sell her child sell him perhaps to certain ruin of body and soul
i am said mr_shelby and i respect your feeling too though i dont pretend to share them to their full extent but i tell you now solemnly it of no use i cant help myself
i didnt mean to tell you this emily but in plain word there is no choice between selling these two and selling everything
no relation however sacred compared with money i sorry you feel so about it indeed either they must go or all must
mr_haley has come into possession of a mortgage which if i dont clear off with him directly will take everything before it
i ve raked and scraped and borrowed and all but begged and the price of these two was needed to make up the balance and i had to give them up
mr_haley fancied the child he agreed to settle the matter that way and no other i was in his power and had to do it
if you feel so to have them sold would it be any better to have all sold mrs mr_shelby stood like one stricken
this is god curse on slavery a bitter bitter most accursed thing a curse to the master and a curse to the slave
finally turning to her toilet she rested her face in her hand and gave a sort of groan i was a fool to think i could make anything good out of such a deadly evil
always thought so when i was a girl i thought so still more after i joined the church but i thought i could gild it over i thought by kindness and care and instruction i could make the condition of mine better than freedom
it is a sin to hold a slave under law like ours i always felt it was i fool that i was why wife you are getting to be an abolitionist quite
we dont need them to tell us you know i never thought that slavery was right never felt willing to own slave
abolitionist if they knew all i know about slavery they might talk well therein you differ from many wise and pious man said mr_shelby
you remember mr s sermon the other sunday i dont want to hear such sermons i never wish to hear mr in our church again
ministers cant help the evil perhaps cant cure it any more than we can but defend it it always went against my common sense
well said mr_shelby i must say these ministers sometimes carry matter further than we poor sinners would exactly dare to do
we man of the world must wink pretty hard at various thing and get used to a deal that isnt the exact thing
but we dont quite fancy when woman and ministers come out broad and square and go beyond us in matter of either modesty or morals that a fact
but now my dear i trust you see the necessity of the thing and you see that i have done the very best that circumstances would allow
o yes yes said mrs mr_shelby hurriedly and abstractedly fingering her gold watch i havent any jewelry of any amount she added thoughtfully
and i think you didnt think much of that sermon either but would not this watch do something it was an expensive one when it was bought
i sorry very sorry emily said mr_shelby i sorry this takes hold of you so but it will do no good
the fact is emily the thing done the bills of sale are already signed and in mr_haley hand and you must be thankful it is no worse
if i could only at least save eliza_harris child i would sacrifice anything i have that man has had it in his power to ruin us
all and now he is fairly off if you knew the man as i do you think that we had had a narrow escape
why not a cruel man exactly but a man of leather a man alive to nothing but trade and profit cool and unhesitating and unrelenting as death and the grave
is he so hard then he sell his own mother at a good percentage not wishing the old woman any harm either
well my dear the fact is that this goes rather hard with me it a thing i hate to think of
and this wretch owns that good faithful tom_loker and eliza_harris child mr_haley wants to drive matter and take possession tomorrow
i going to get out my horse bright and early and be off i cant see tom_loker that a fact and you had better arrange a drive somewhere and carry eliza_harris off
let the thing be done when she is out of sight no no said mrs mr_shelby i ll be in no sense accomplice or help in this cruel business
i ll go and see poor old tom_loker god help him in his distress they shall see at any rate that their mistress can feel for and with them
as to eliza_harris i dare not think about it the lord forgive us what have we done that this cruel necessity should come on us
there was one listener to this conversation whom mr and mrs mr_shelby little suspected communicating with their apartment was a large closet opening by a door into the outer passage
when mrs mr_shelby had dismissed eliza_harris for the night her feverish and excited mind had suggested the idea of this closet and she had hidden herself there and with her ear pressed close against the crack of the door had lost not a word of the conversation
pale shivering with rigid features and compressed lips she looked an entirely altered being from the soft and timid creature she had been hitherto
she moved cautiously along the entry paused one moment at her mistress door and raised her hand in mute appeal to heaven and then turned and glided into her own room
when the voice died into silence she rose and crept stealthily away it was a quiet neat apartment on the same floor with her mistress
there was a pleasant sunny window where she had often sat singing at her sewing there a little case of book and various little fancy articles ranged by them the gifts of christmas holidays there was her simple wardrobe in the closet and in the drawers here was in short her home and on the whole a happy one it had been to her
but there on the bed lay her slumbering boy his long curls falling negligently around his unconscious face his rosy mouth half open his little fat hand thrown out over the bedclothes and a smile spread like a sunbeam over his whole face
no tear dropped over that pillow in such straits as these the heart has no tear to give it drops only blood bleeding itself away in silence
poor boy poor fellow said eliza_harris they have sold you but your mother will save you yet she took a piece of paper and a pencil and wrote hastily missis
dear missis dont think me ungrateful dont think hard of me any way i heard all you and master said tonight i am going to try to save my boy you will not blame me
hastily folding and directing this she went to a drawer and made up a little package of clothing for her boy which she tied with a handkerchief firmly round her waist and so fond is a mother remembrance that even in the terrors of that hour she did not forget to put in the little package one or two of his favorite toys reserving a gayly painted parrot to amuse him when she should be called on to awaken him
it was some trouble to arouse the little sleeper but after some effort he sat up and was playing with his mrs_bird while his mother was putting on her bonnet and shawl
god bless and reward you for all your kindness where are you going mother said he as she drew near the bed with his little coat and cap
his mother drew near and looked so earnestly into his eye that he at once divined that something unusual was the matter
a wicked man was coming to take little harry away from his mother and carry him way off in the dark but mother wont let him
she going to put on her little boy cap and coat and run off with him so the ugly man cant catch him
saying these word she had tied and buttoned on the child simple outfit and taking him in her arm she whispered to him to be very still and opening a door in her room which led into the outer verandah she glided noiselessly out
it was a sparkling frosty starlight night and the mother wrapped the shawl close round her child as perfectly quiet with vague terror he clung round her neck
old bruno a great newfoundland who slept at the end of the porch rose with a low growl as she came near
she gently spoke his name and the animal an old pet and playmate of hers instantly wagging his tail prepared to follow her though apparently revolving much in this simple dog head what such an indiscreet midnight promenade might mean
some dim ideas of imprudence or impropriety in the measure seemed to embarrass him considerably for he often stopped as eliza_harris glided forward and looked wistfully first at her and then at the house and then as if reassured by reflection he pattered along after her again
hush harry she said mustnt speak loud or they will hear us a few minutes brought them to the window of uncle tom_loker cottage and eliza_harris stopping tapped lightly on the window pane
the prayer meeting at uncle tom_loker had in the order of hymn singing been protracted to a very late hour and as uncle tom_loker had indulged himself in a few lengthy solos afterwards the consequence was that although it was now between twelve and one clock he and his worthy helpmeet were not yet asleep
good lord what that said aunt_chloe starting up and hastily drawing the curtain my sakes alive if it ant lizy
get on your clothes old man quick there old bruno too a pawin round what on airth i gwine to open the door
and suiting the action to the word the door flew open and the light of the tallow candle which tom_loker had hastily lighted fell on the haggard face and dark wild eye of the fugitive
lord bless you i skeered to look at ye lizy are ye tuck sick or what come over ye i running away uncle tom_loker and aunt_chloe carrying off my child master sold him
yes sold him said eliza_harris firmly i crept into the closet by mistress door tonight and i heard master tell missis that he had sold my harry and you uncle tom_loker both to a trader and that he was going off this morning on his horse and that the man was to take possession today
sold him echoed both lifting up their hand in dismay tom_loker had stood during this speech with his hand raised and his eye dilated like a man in a dream
slowly and gradually as its meaning came over him he collapsed rather than seated himself on his old chair and sunk his head down upon his knees
the good lord have pity on us said aunt_chloe it dont seem as if it was true
what has he done that mas should sell him he hasnt done anything it isnt for that master dont want to sell and missis
i heard her plead and beg for us but he told hert was no use that he was in this man debt and that this man had got the power over him and that if he didnt pay him off clear it would end in his having to sell the place and all the people and move off
yes i heard him say there was no choice between selling these two and selling all the man was driving him so hard
she always good master said he was sorry but oh missis you ought to have heard her talk if she ant a christian and an angel there never was one
she said herself one soul was worth more than the world and this boy has a soul and if i let him be carried off who knows what ll become of it
i a wicked girl to leave her so but then i cant help it it must be right but if it ant right the lord forgive me for i cant help doing it
well old man said aunt_chloe why dont you go too will you wait to be toted down river where they kill nigger with hard work and starving
i a heap rather die than go there any day there time for ye be off with lizy you ve got a pass to come and go any time
come bustle up and i ll get your thing together tom_loker slowly raised his head and looked sorrowfully but quietly around and said no no i ant going
let eliza_harris go it her right i wouldnt be the one to say no tant in natur for her to stay but you heard what she said
if i must be sold or all the people on the place and everything go to rack why let me be sold
i pose i can bar it as well as any on em he added while something like a sob and a sigh shook his broad rough chest convulsively
mas always found me on the spot he always will i never have broke trust nor used my pass no way contrary to my word and i never will
it better for me alone to go than to break up the place and sell all mas ant to blame aunt_chloe and he ll take care of you and the poor
here he turned to the rough trundle bed full of little woolly head and broke fairly down he leaned over the back of the chair and covered his face with his large hand
sobs heavy hoarse and loud shook the chair and great tear fell through his fingers on the floor just such tear sir as you dropped into the coffin where lay your first born son such tear woman as you shed when you heard the cries of your dying babe
and woman though dressed in silk and jewels you are but a woman and in life great straits and mighty griefs ye feel but one sorrow
and now said eliza_harris as she stood in the door i saw my husband only this afternoon and i little knew then what was to come
they have pushed him to the very last standing place and he told me today that he was going to run away
for sir he was a man and you are but another man do try if you can to get word to him
you must give my love to him and tell him if i never see him again she turned away and stood with her back to them for a moment and then added in a husky voice tell him to be as good as he can and try and meet me in the kingdom of heaven
tell him how i went and why i went and tell him i going to try and find canada call bruno in there she added
a few last word and tear a few simple adieus and blessings and clasping her wondering and affrighted child in her arm she glided noiselessly away
chapter vi discovery mr and mrs mr_shelby after their protracted discussion of the night before did not readily sink to repose and in consequence slept somewhat later than usual the ensuing morning
shut the door on him poor beast he mustnt go with me i wonder what keeps eliza_harris said mrs mr_shelby after giving her bell repeated pulls to no purpose
mr_shelby was standing before his dressing glass sharpening his razor and just then the door opened and a colored boy entered with his shaving water
